msg:I can only say that maybe my expectations were too high, and Yiyang was the best recommended by Ctrip.
The external environment is poorly maintained!
I stayed in the internal room for many days. I took the initiative to ask not to change the bed linen, but the room was not cleaned (the tissue box on the washstand was open, but the tissue was not put in; the trash bag in the room trash can was changed, but the empty bottles next to it were not taken away; the disposable slippers were not put in until they were asked for every day...) Of course, not all cleaning staff are so sloppy. Later, there was an aunt whose work ID card I took a special photo of. She was quick and talkative, and corrected the previous shortcomings!
Regarding breakfast, I first give a thumbs up to the guy who checked in on the first day. The child was 12 years old, but he was tall. He still took the initiative to adjust it to half price. A few dozen yuan was a small matter. The warm-hearted move added points to the initial impression! In addition, the aunt who cooked noodles was always busy but smiled and was friendly, which made people not annoyed even if they were queuing! Speaking of the service staff at the door of the restaurant, their professionalism and adaptability need to be improved!
In and out of the hotel, from the security guard at the entrance to the staff who looked like managers walking around in the lobby, no one took the initiative to say hello, they all passed by with expressionless faces! 
I have said too much, and finally I will silently add another star to encourage you. I hope you will get better and better!
